    17: }

    19: function aiwB6R96R1G2FirstText(values) {
    20:   for (const value of values) {

    22:     if (text) return text;
    23:   }
    24:   return "";

   552: function loadDotEnv(filePath) {
   553:   if (!fs.existsSync(filePath)) return;
   554:   const lines = fs.readFileSync(filePath, "utf8").split(/\r?\n/);

   557:     const idx = line.indexOf("=");

   560:     const value = line.slice(idx + 1).trim();
   561:     if (key && process.env[key] === undefined) {
   562:       process.env[key] = value;
   563:     }
   564:   }
   565: }

   301: function aiwB6R96R1G2BuildRequesterDeliveryPayload(payload) {

   327:     summary_text: role + " role produced a stable minimum deliverable.",

   745: function deliveryBoard(query) {
   746:   return psqlJson(`
   747:     select coalesce(jsonb_agg(to_jsonb(t) order by created_at desc), '[]'::jsonb)::text
   748:     from (
   749:       select *
   750:       from aiworker.vw_app_aiworker_runtime_delivery_board_v1
   751:       where (nullif(:'request_id','') is null or request_id::text = :'request_id')
   752:         and (nullif(:'request_code','') is null or request_code = :'request_code')
   753:       order by created_at desc
   754:       limit :'limit'
   755:     ) t;
   756:   `, {
   757:     request_id: query.get("request_id") || "",
   758:     request_code: query.get("request_code") || "",
   759:     limit: normalizeLimit(query.get("limit"))
   760:   });
   761: }

  1774: const server = http.createServer(async (req, res) => {
  1775:   const url = new URL(req.url, `http://${req.headers.host || "127.0.0.1"}`);
  1776: 
  1777:   try {
  1778:     if (req.method === "GET" && url.pathname === "/health") {
  1779:       return sendJson(res, 200, {
  1780:         ok: true,
  1781:         service: "aiworker-runtime-execution-http-api",
  1782:         db: "PERSONA_DATABASE_URL",
  1783:         external_execution: false,
  1784:         pg_apply: false,
  1785:         destructive_action: false
  1786:       });
  1787:     }
  1788: 
  1789:     if (!requireAuth(req)) {
  1790:       return sendJson(res, 401, {
  1791:         result: "error",
  1792:         error_code: "UNAUTHORIZED",
  1793:         message: "Missing or invalid Authorization bearer token."
  1794:       });
  1795:     }
  1796: 
  1797:     if (req.method === "GET" && url.pathname === "/aiworker/v1/runtime-execution/endpoint-ready") {
  1798:       return sendJson(res, 200, { result: "ok", data: endpointReady() });
  1799:     }
  1800: 
  1801:     if (req.method === "GET" && url.pathname === "/aiworker/v1/runtime-execution/api-contract") {
  1802:       return sendJson(res, 200, { result: "ok", data: apiContracts() });
  1803:     }
  1804: 
  1805:     if (req.method === "GET" && url.pathname === "/aiworker/v1/runtime-execution/persistent-smoke") {
  1806:       return sendJson(res, 200, { result: "ok", data: persistentSmoke() });
  1807:     }
  1808: 
  1809:     if (req.method === "GET" && url.pathname === "/aiworker/v1/runtime-execution/pipeline-board") {
  1810:       return sendJson(res, 200, { result: "ok", data: pipelineBoard(url.searchParams) });
  1811:     }
  1812: 
  1813:     if (req.method === "GET" && url.pathname === "/aiworker/v1/runtime-execution/app-read-payload") {
  1814:       return sendJson(res, 200, { result: "ok", data: appReadPayload(url.searchParams) });
  1815:     }
  1816: 
  1817:     if (req.method === "GET" && url.pathname === "/aiworker/v1/runtime-execution/delivery") {
  1818:       return sendJson(res, 200, { result: "ok", data: deliveryBoard(url.searchParams) });
  1819:     }
  1820: 
  1821:

   301: function aiwB6R96R1G2BuildRequesterDeliveryPayload(payload) {
   302:   payload = aiwB6R96R1G2Object(payload);
   303:   const appPayload = aiwB6R96R1G2FindAppPayload(payload);
   304: 
   305:   const title = aiwB6R96R1G2FirstText([
   306:     aiwB6R96R1G2Pick(payload, ["task_title", "title", "request_title"]),
   307:     aiwB6R96R1G2Pick(appPayload, ["task_title", "title", "request_title"]),
   308:     "AIWorkerOS成果物"
   309:   ]);
   310: 
   311:   const instruction = aiwB6R96R1G2FirstText([
   312:     aiwB6R96R1G2Pick(payload, ["task_instruction_ja", "instruction", "prompt", "task_description"]),
   313:     aiwB6R96R1G2Pick(appPayload, ["task_instruction_ja", "instruction", "prompt", "task_description"])
   314:   ]);
   315: 
   316:   const role = aiwB6R96R1G2NormalizeRoleCode(payload, appPayload);
   317:   const tier = aiwB6R96R1G2CapabilityTier(payload, appPayload);
   318:   const referenceProfile = aiwB6R96R1G2ReferenceProfile(tier);
   319:   const body = aiwB6R96R1G2BuildBody(role, title, instruction, referenceProfile);
   320: 
   321:   return {
   322:     contract_version: "requester_deliverable_v1",
   323:     deliverable_title: title,
   324:     deliverable_kind: role === "president" ? "policy_proposal" : role === "manager" ? "major_breakdown" : role === "leader" ? "task_decomposition" : "document",
   325:     body_format: "markdown",
   326:     body_markdown: body,
   327:     summary_text: role + " role produced a stable minimum deliverable.",
   328:     limitations_text: "Performance differences are controlled by CX reference permission and capability profile. Low performance still returns stable output.",
   329:     unresolved_issues_text: instruction ? "" : "Task instruction is missing or insufficient.",
   330:     next_steps_text: "Review the deliverable and provide additional constraints if deeper specialty or originality is required.",
   331:     minimum_guarantee_status: body ? "satisfied" : "blocking_report",
   332:     performance_profile: {
   333:       capability_tier: tier,
   334:       stability_level: referenceProfile.stability_level,
   335:       originality_level: referenceProfile.originality_level,
   336:       specialty_level: referenceProfile.specialty_level,
   337:       prediction_level: referenceProfile.prediction_level,
   338:       review_depth: referenceProfile.review_depth
   339:     },
   340:     reference_usage_profile: referenceProfile,
   341:     generation_basis: {
   342:       role_code: role,
   343:       task_title: title,
   344:       has_instruction: Boolean(instruction),
   345:       generated_by: "AIW_B6R96R1G2_MINIMUM_DELIVERABLE_HELPER"
   346:     }
   347:   };
   348: }

   350: function aiwB6R96R1G2EnsureRequesterDeliveryPayload(payload) {
   351:   if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object" || Array.isArray(payload)) return payload;
   352: 
   353:   const current = aiwB6R96R1G2Object(payload.requester_delivery_payload);
   354:   if (aiwB6R96R1G2Text(current.body_markdown) || aiwB6R96R1G2Text(current.body_text)) {
   355:     return payload;
   356:   }
   357: 
   358:   if (!aiwB6R96R1G2LooksRuntimePayload(payload)) return payload;
   359: 
   360:   payload.requester_delivery_payload = aiwB6R96R1G2BuildRequesterDeliveryPayload(payload);
   361:   payload.deliverable = payload.requester_delivery_payload;
   362:   return payload;
   363: }

   366: function aiwB6R44fPlainObject(value) {
   367:   return value && typeof value === "object" && !Array.isArray(value) ? value : {};
   368: }
   369: 
   370: function aiwB6R44fText(value) {
   371:   return value == null ? "" : String(value).trim();
   372: }
   373: 
   374: function aiwB6R44fExtractSourceRouteMetadata(input) {
   375:   const body = aiwB6R44fPlainObject(input);
   376:   const metadata = aiwB6R44fPlainObject(body.metadata_jsonb);
   377:   const appRead = aiwB6R44fPlainObject(body.app_read_payload_jsonb);
   378:   const source = aiwB6R44fPlainObject(appRead.source);
   379: 
   380:   const sourceAppRef = aiwB6R44fText(
   381:     body.source_app_ref ||
   382:     metadata.source_app_ref ||
   383:     source.source_app_ref ||
   384:     body.app_surface_code ||
   385:     "AICompanyManager"
   386:   );
   387: 
   388:   const sourceRouteCode = aiwB6R44fText(
   389:     body.source_route_code ||
   390:     metadata.source_route_code ||
   391:     source.source_route_code
   392:   );
   393: 
   394:   const sourceScreenCode = aiwB6R44fText(
   395:     body.source_screen_code ||
   396:     metadata.source_screen_code ||
   397:     source.source_screen_code
   398:   );
   399: 
   400:   const sourceEntityType = aiwB6R44fText(
   401:     body.source_entity_type ||
   402:     metadata.source_entity_type ||
   403:     source.source_entity_type
   404:   );
   405: 
   406:   const sourceEntityId = aiwB6R44fText(
   407:     body.source_entity_id ||
   408:     metadata.source_entity_id ||
   409:     source.source_entity_id ||
   410:     body.request_id ||
   411:     body.runtime_execution_request_id
   412:   );
   413: 
   414:   const route = {};
   415:   if (sourceAppRef) route.source_app_ref = sourceAppRef;
   416:   if (sourceRouteCode) route.source_route_code = sourceRouteCode;
   417:   if (sourceScreenCode) route.source_screen_code = sourceScreenCode;
   418:   if (sourceEntityType) route.source_entity_type = sourceEntityType;
   419:   if (sourceEntityId) route.source_entity_id = sourceEntityId;
   420: 
   421:   const returnTargetType = aiwB6R44fText(body.return_target_type || metadata.return_target_type || source.return_target_type);
   422:   const returnTargetId = aiwB6R44fText(body.return_target_id || metadata.return_target_id || source.return_target_id);
   423:   const reexecuteTargetType = aiwB6R44fText(body.reexecute_target_type || metadata.reexecute_target_type || source.reexecute_target_type);
   424:   const reexecuteTargetId = aiwB6R44fText(body.reexecute_target_id || metadata.reexecute_target_id || source.reexecute_target_id);
   425:   const contextRestoreType = aiwB6R44fText(body.context_restore_type || metadata.context_restore_type || source.context_restore_type);
   426:   const contextRestoreId = aiwB6R44fText(body.context_restore_id || metadata.context_restore_id || source.context_restore_id);
   427: 
   428:   if (returnTargetType) route.return_target_type = returnTargetType;
   429:   if (returnTargetId) route.return_target_id = returnTargetId;
   430:   if (reexecuteTargetType) route.reexecute_target_type = reexecuteTargetType;
   431:   if (reexecuteTargetId) route.reexecute_target_id = reexecuteTargetId;
   432:   if (contextRestoreType) route.context_restore_type = contextRestoreType;
   433:   if (contextRestoreId) route.context_restore_id = contextRestoreId;
   434: 
   435:   return route;
   436: }
   437: 
   438: function aiwB6R44fMergeSourceRouteIntoAppReadPayload(appReadPayload, input) {
   439:   const base = aiwB6R44fPlainObject(appReadPayload);
   440:   const route = aiwB6R44fExtractSourceRouteMetadata(input);
   441:   if (!route.source_route_code) return base;
   442:   return Object.assign({}, base, {
   443:     source: Object.assign({}, aiwB6R44fPlainObject(base.source), route)
   444:   });
   445: }
   446: 
   447: function aiwB6R44fExposeSourceRouteOnRow(row) {
   448:   const out = Object.assign({}, aiwB6R44fPlainObject(row));
   449:   const appRead = aiwB6R44fPlainObject(out.app_read_payload_jsonb);
   450:   const source = aiwB6R44fPlainObject(appRead.source);
   451:   const route = aiwB6R44fExtractSourceRouteMetadata(Object.assign({}, out, {
   452:     metadata_jsonb: out.metadata_jsonb,
   453:     app_read_payload_jsonb: aiwB6R44fMergeSourceRouteIntoAppReadPayload(appRead, body || payload || requestBody || input || {}),
   454:     source_app_ref: out.source_app_ref || source.source_app_ref,
   455:     source_route_code: out.source_route_code || source.source_route_code,
   456:     source_screen_code: out.source_screen_code || source.source_screen_code,
   457:     source_entity_type: out.source_entity_type || source.source_entity_type,
   458:     source_entity_id: out.source_entity_id || source.source_entity_id
   459:   }));
   460: 
   461:   if (route.source_app_ref && !out.source_app_ref) out.source_app_ref = route.source_app_ref;
   462:   if (route.source_route_code && !out.source_route_code) out.source_route_code = route.source_route_code;
   463:   if (route.source_screen_code && !out.source_screen_code) out.source_screen_code = route.source_screen_code;
   464:   if (route.source_entity_type && !out.source_entity_type) out.source_entity_type = route.source_entity_type;
   465:   if (route.source_entity_id && !out.source_entity_id) out.source_entity_id = route.source_entity_id;
   466: 
   467:   if (route.source_route_code) {
   468:     out.app_read_payload_jsonb = aiwB6R44fMergeSourceRouteIntoAppReadPayload(appRead, route);
   469:   }
   470:   return out;
   471: }
   472: 
   473: function aiwB6R44fExposeSourceRouteOnRows(value) {
   474:   if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.map(aiwB6R44fExposeSourceRouteOnRow);
   475:   return value;
   476: }

   552: function loadDotEnv(filePath) {
   553:   if (!fs.existsSync(filePath)) return;
   554:   const lines = fs.readFileSync(filePath, "utf8").split(/\r?\n/);
   555:   for (const line of lines) {
   556:     if (!line || line.trim().startsWith("#")) continue;
   557:     const idx = line.indexOf("=");
   558:     if (idx < 0) continue;
   559:     const key = line.slice(0, idx).trim();
   560:     const value = line.slice(idx + 1).trim();
   561:     if (key && process.env[key] === undefined) {
   562:       process.env[key] = value;
   563:     }
   564:   }
   565: }

   598: function readBody(req) {
   599:   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   600:     let body = "";
   601:     req.on("data", chunk => {
   602:       body += chunk;
   603:       if (body.length > 1024 * 1024) {
   604:         reject(new Error("Request body too large"));
   605:         req.destroy();
   606:       }
   607:     });
   608:     req.on("end", () => resolve(body));
   609:     req.on("error", reject);
   610:   });
   611: }

   613: function requireAuth(req) {
   614:   const auth = req.headers["authorization"] || "";
   615:   return auth === `Bearer ${authToken}`;
   616: }

   618: function normalizeLimit(value) {
   619:   const n = Number(value || "20");
   620:   if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return 20;
   621:   return Math.max(1, Math.min(100, Math.floor(n)));
   622: }

   626:  * Do not pass SQL using `psql -c` here.

   629:  *
   630:  * This fixed version passes SQL via stdin.

   632: function psqlJson(sql, vars = {}) {

   552: function loadDotEnv(filePath) {
   553:   if (!fs.existsSync(filePath)) return;
   554:   const lines = fs.readFileSync(filePath, "utf8").split(/\r?\n/);
   555:   for (const line of lines) {
   556:     if (!line || line.trim().startsWith("#")) continue;
   557:     const idx = line.indexOf("=");
   558:     if (idx < 0) continue;
   559:     const key = line.slice(0, idx).trim();
   560:     const value = line.slice(idx + 1).trim();
   561:     if (key && process.env[key] === undefined) {
   562:       process.env[key] = value;
   563:     }
   564:   }
   565: }

   598: function readBody(req) {
   599:   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   600:     let body = "";
   601:     req.on("data", chunk => {
   602:       body += chunk;
   603:       if (body.length > 1024 * 1024) {
   604:         reject(new Error("Request body too large"));
   605:         req.destroy();
   606:       }
   607:     });
   608:     req.on("end", () => resolve(body));
   609:     req.on("error", reject);
   610:   });

   632: function psqlJson(sql, vars = {}) {
   633:   const args = [
   634:     databaseUrl,
   635:     "-X",
   636:     "-A",
   637:     "-t",
   638:     "-v",
   639:     "ON_ERROR_STOP=1"
   640:   ];
   641: 
   642:   for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(vars)) {
   643:     args.push("-v", `${key}=${value === null || value === undefined ? "" : String(value)}`);
   644:   }
   645: 
   646:   const result = spawnSync("psql", args, {
   647:     input: sql,
   648:     encoding: "utf8",
   649:     maxBuffer: 1024 * 1024 * 20
   650:   });
   651: 
   652:   if (result.status !== 0) {
   653:     const message = result.stderr || result.stdout || "psql failed";
   654:     const err = new Error(message.trim());
   655:     err.stderr = result.stderr;
   656:     err.stdout = result.stdout;
   657:     err.status = result.status;
   658:     throw err;
   659:   }
   660: 
   661:   const text = (result.stdout || "").trim();
   662:   if (!text) return null;
   663: 
   664:   try {
   665:     return JSON.parse(text);
   666:   } catch (e) {
   667:     throw new Error(`Failed to parse DB JSON: ${text}`);
   668:   }
   669: }

  1120: function aiwB6R95R3Z24RunPsqlJson(sql) {

  1123:     req = eval("require");
  1124:   } catch {
  1125:     return [];
  1126:   }
  1127: 
  1128:   try {

  1145:       timeout: 15000,

  1147:     });
  1148:

  1150:     if (!text) return [];
  1151:     const parsed = JSON.parse(text);
  1152:     return Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [];
  1153:   } catch {
  1154:     return [];
  1155:   }
